# Feature Matrix (Source of Truth)

Last audited: 2026-03-06  
Owner: Product + Engineering

## Purpose

Single artifact to track feature implementation state and delivery completeness across IntelliFlow CRM.

This matrix is the canonical view for:
- Feature status (`planned`, `in_progress`, `done`)
- Requirement traceability (`Related Task (CSV)`, `Flow Ref`, task-scoped `PRD Ref` / `ADR Ref`, `Shared Context Ref`)
- End-to-end chain coverage
  (`Entity -> Domain -> Database -> Adapter -> Router -> Frontend-List/Detail + Events/Security gates`)
- Validation sources (`KPI`, `Validation Method`, evidence artifacts)
- Missing CSV tasks needed to fully plan or complete a feature

## Status Rubric

| Status | Definition |
|---|---|
| `done` | Implemented and wired to active data/API paths for the primary user flow |
| `in_progress` | Partially implemented, mock/placeholder behavior, or known integration gaps |
| `planned` | Backlog item with no production-ready flow yet |

### Wiring Status (Audit Overlay)

Wiring status is determined by entity detail wiring audits (2026-03-03 to 2026-03-06).
Audited entities: Lead, Contact, Account, Deal.

| Wiring Status | Definition |
|---|---|
| `verified` | Audit-confirmed: wiring is functional end-to-end for the primary user flow |
| `issues` | Audit found defects: functional but with gaps (no-op buttons, missing handlers, security issues) |
| `unaudited` | Feature is `done` but has not yet been audited for wiring correctness |
| `-` | Not applicable (feature is `planned`/`in_progress`, or group not yet audited) |

Audit documents: `docs/audit/{lead,contact,account,deal}-detail-wiring-audit.md`
Cross-reference: `docs/audit/feature-matrix-vs-audit-comparison.md`

## Completeness Rubric

| Plan Coverage | Definition |
|---|---|
| `complete` | All required layers for this feature type are covered by CSV tasks |
| `partial` | 1-2 required layers are missing tasks |
| `gap` | 3+ required layers are missing tasks |
| `at_risk` | Feature is `done` or `in_progress` but still has missing required layers |

Forecast risk rubric:
- `critical` = `done` with unresolved dependencies, missing dependency references, or missing artifact paths
- `high` = `in_progress` with dependency/path issues, or major layer risk
- `medium` = non-critical row with partial layer risk
- `low` = no immediate leading indicators of delivery slippage

Doc-linking criteria:
- `PRD Ref` / `ADR Ref` include only task-scoped evidence (task ID or feature/title mention in the document)
- Range-only or generic docs are listed in `Shared Context Ref` to avoid masking row-level documentation gaps

Layer cell legend:
- `not_required` = layer is not required for this feature type
- `missing` = required layer has no linked CSV task
- `done/in_progress/planned/partial (N task(s))` = layer has linked task

Quality gate legend (Events / Security columns):

- `verified` = audit-confirmed functional
- `issues (detail)` = audit found non-critical defects
- `critical (detail)` = audit found CRITICAL security/data issues
- `partial (N/M handlers)` = some event handlers implemented
- `not-wired (0/M handlers)` = events defined but zero handlers registered
- `not_required` = quality gate not applicable for this feature type
- `unaudited` = not yet audited

## Coverage Snapshot

- Route-backed product surfaces: 68 pages (`docs/design/sitemap.md`)
- CSV-linked PG tasks covered: 179
- CSV-linked IFC capabilities covered: 286
- Other CSV capability tasks covered: 68
- Total feature entries: 629
- Groups covered: 22
- Plan coverage: complete=566, partial=11, gap=50, at_risk=2
- Missing required layers (count of features):
  - Entity: 51
  - Domain: 48
  - Database: 49
  - Adapter: 52
  - Router: 23
  - Frontend: 0
  - Frontend-List: 0
  - Frontend-Detail: 0
  - Events: n/a (quality gate)
  - Security: n/a (quality gate)

## Maintenance Rules

1. Update this matrix in the same PR whenever a feature status changes.
2. Update `Related Task (CSV)` whenever task IDs or dependencies change in `apps/project-tracker/docs/metrics/_global/Sprint_plan.csv`.
3. Keep `Flow Ref`, task-scoped `PRD Ref` / `ADR Ref`, and `Shared Context Ref` updated as source docs are created or updated.
4. For any `Missing CSV Task(s)` entry, add task(s) to `Sprint_plan.csv` and replace the gap in the same PR.
5. Keep status values limited to `planned`, `in_progress`, `done`.
